***wieberen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wieberen.html>wieberen</a> (48055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wieberig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> ~ <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a> / ~ <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>: (Bargoens) </i>to scarper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i> lt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">ועייִבערעח</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veyiverekh</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> lt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">וַיִּבְרַח</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vayivrách</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(he) fled</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wieberen.html>wieberen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scarper, to flee</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go, to move</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move, to remove</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay off</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Often used in the imperative infinitive, often with a negative charge, as in: ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:sod.html>Sod</a> off!’ Also used to indicate wavering, uncertain, amp;c. motion. Nowadays also used transitively, in which case the active <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> formed using the auxiliary verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wieberen.html>wieberen</a></b>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:weggaan.html>weggaan</a></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wied.html>wied</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unwanted plant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wiod</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weudą</i>. ***wiel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiel.html>wiel</a> (6111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiel.html>wiel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wiol</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwehwlą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷekʷlóm</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷékʷlos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiel.html>wiel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

</p>
<ol><li>a sports or fitness cyclist, someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:races.html>races</a> bicycles, as opposed to a person riding a bike for any other purpose. <span class="defdate">[from ca. 1889]</span></li></ol>

</p>

***wiens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a> (1816)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Genitive masculine singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>Wiens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Whose car <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Martin <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buren.html>Buren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> Amerikaanse president <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:moedertaal.html>moedertaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>Engels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> Nederlands.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Martin <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buren.html>Buren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only American president whose mother tongue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not English. His first language <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> Dutch.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>Wiens</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> come to replace its female equivalent, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i>, in both singular and plural. While <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the genitive masculine singular of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the genitive feminine singular and the genitive plural. Although the use of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> become largely archaic and dialectal, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still recommended by grammarians. Example sentences of different usage:
</p>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> president <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wiens.html>wiens</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:moedertaal.html>moedertaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>Engels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.  |  <i>He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only president whose mother tongue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not English.</i> (genitive masculine singular)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:presidente.html>presidente</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:moedertaal.html>moedertaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>Engels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.  |  <i>She <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only president whose mother tongue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not English.</i> (genitive feminine singular)</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:presidenten.html>presidenten</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:moedertaal.html>moedertaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:engels.html>Engels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.  |  <i>They are the only presidents whose mother tongue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not English.</i> (genitive plural)</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>, <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">mv</span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen_2"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>, <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">mv</span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></li></ul>

***wier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a> (12647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seaweed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly descended through Old Dutch from Proto-Germanic, or <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from Frisian. Cognate with dialectal English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ware.html>ware</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seaweed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">war</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seaweed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wiertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>seaweed</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Before the 18th century, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> sometimes considered to be feminine.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">seaweed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alg.html>alg</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">alge</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">zeegras</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">groenwieren</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeewier.html>zeewier</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> whose (feminine, plural)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wierooc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīrōk</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">*wīh</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">holy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīhaz</i>) + <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">rouc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rōk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raukiz</i>).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiet.html>wiet</a> (3465)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">weed</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marijuana</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">weed</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wēod</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weudą</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wied.html>wied</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unwanted plant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***wight.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a> (52689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wiȝt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wiht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a>, person, creature, being, <a href = vnd.unilang:whit.html>whit</a>, thing, something, anything</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wihtiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">essence, object</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wekti-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cause, sake, thing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wekʷ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to say, tell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">creature, being, human</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">child, <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>Wicht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">girl; <a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>Wicht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wretch, <a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a>, little creature, scoundrel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bokm%C3%A5l" class="extiw" title="w:Bokmål">Norwegian Bokmål</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nb"><a href = vnd.unilang:vette.html>vette</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">underground creature, gnome</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">vätte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">underground creature, gnome</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">vættur</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">imp, <a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whit.html>whit</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">wights</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A living creature, especially a human being.
<ul><li><b>circa 1602</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Merry_Wives_of_Windsor" class="extiw" title="s:The Merry Wives of Windsor">The Merry <a href = vnd.unilang:wives.html>Wives</a> of Windsor</a></i>, act 1, scene 3:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> base Hungarian <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b>! <a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a> thou the spigot wield?</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1626</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Milton">John Milton</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/On_the_Death_of_a_Fair_Infant_Dying_of_a_Cough" class="extiw" title="s:On the Death of a Fair Infant Dying of a Cough">On the Death of a Fair Infant Dying of a Cough</a></i>, verse vi
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a> say <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> true if thou wert mortal <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b><br />And why from us so quickly thou didst take thy flight.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1851</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moby_Dick" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Moby Dick"><a href = vnd.unilang:moby.html>Moby</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>Dick</a></a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/ebooks/2701">[1]</a></sup>, chapter 14:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Some gamesome <b>wights</b> will tell you that they have to plant weeds there, they don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> grow naturally; [...]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>circa 1872</b>, a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Knight%27s_tour" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Knight | s tour">Knight's tour</a> cryptotour poem, possibly by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Howard_Staunton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Howard Staunton">Howard Staunton</a>, lines 1 and 2:
<dl><dd>"The <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> that hath no love of chess/<a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> truth to say a <a href = vnd.unilang:sorry.html>sorry</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b>."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1885</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_F._Burton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Richard F. Burton">Richard F. Burton</a>, <i>The Supplemental <a href = vnd.unilang:nights.html>Nights</a> to the Thousand <a href = vnd.unilang:nights.html>Nights</a> and a Night</i>, Night 532:
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>Alaeddin <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>ate</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:drank.html>drank</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> cheered and after he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> rested and <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> recovered <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a> he cried, "<a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>Ah</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> my mother, I have a sore grievance against <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a> for leaving <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to that accursed <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> who strave to compass my destruction and designed to take my life. Know that I beheld Death with mine own <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> at the hand of this damned wretch, whom thou didst certify to be my uncle;<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">paganism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A being of one of the Nine Worlds of Heathen belief, especially a nature spirit, <a href = vnd.unilang:elf.html>elf</a> or ancestor.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A ghost, deity or other supernatural entity.
<ul><li><b>1789</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Blake" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Blake">William <a href = vnd.unilang:blake.html>Blake</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/A_Dream_(Blake)" class="extiw" title="s:A Dream (Blake)">A Dream</a></i>, lines 14-16:
<dl><dd>But I saw a glow-worm near, / Who replied: ‘What wailing <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> / Calls the watchman of the night?</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1851</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moby_Dick" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Moby Dick"><a href = vnd.unilang:moby.html>Moby</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>Dick</a></a></cite>, chapter 2:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“In judging of that tempestuous wind called Euroclydon,” says an old writer—of whose works I possess the only copy extant—“it maketh a marvellous difference, whether thou lookest out at it from a glass window where the frost <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> all on the outside, or whether thou observest it from that sashless window, where the frost <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on both sides, and of which the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> Death <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only glazier.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1869</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Morris" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Morris">William Morris</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eir%C3%ADkr_Magn%C3%BAsson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Eiríkr Magnússon">Eiríkr Magnússon</a> (translators), <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grettis_Saga" class="extiw" title="w:Grettis Saga">Grettis Saga: The Story of Grettir the Strong</a></i>, F. S. Ellis, page 49:
<dl><dd>Everything in their way <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> kicked out of place, the barrow-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> setting on with hideous eagerness; Grettir <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> back before him for a long time, till at last it <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to this, that he saw it would not do to hoard his strength any more; now neither spared the other, and they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> to where the horse-bones <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a>, and thereabout they wrestled long.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">fantasy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A wraith-like creature.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">vígt</i>, neuter of <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">vígr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skilled in fighting, of age</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīgaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fighting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyk-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wīġ</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> except in dialects</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:brave.html>Brave</a>, valorous, strong.
<ul><li><b>1485</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Malory" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Malory">Thomas Malory</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://quod.lib.umich.edu/c/cme/MaloryWks2/1:20.9?rgn=div2;view=fulltext">chapter ix</a>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Le_Morte_d%27Arthur" class="extiw" title="w:Le Morte d | Arthur">Le <a href = vnd.unilang:morte.html>Morte</a> Darthur</a></i>, book XVIII:
<dl><dd>I haue two sones that <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> but late made knyghtes / and the eldest hyghte <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a> Tirre /<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>/ and my yongest sone hyght Lauayne / and yf hit please <a href = vnd.unilang:yow.html>yow</a> / he shalle ryde with <a href = vnd.unilang:yow.html>yow</a> vnto that Iustes / and he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> of his age x stronge and <b>wyght</b></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Strong; <a href = vnd.unilang:stout.html>stout</a>; active.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="ante">a.</abbr></i> <b>1450</b>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robin_Hood_and_the_Monk" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robin Hood and the Monk"><a href = vnd.unilang:robin.html>Robin</a> Hood and the Monk</a>”, in Sidgwick, <a href = vnd.unilang:frank.html>Frank</a>, editor, <cite><a href="http://www.gutenberg.org/etext/28744" class="extiw" title="gutenberg:28744">Ballads of <a href = vnd.unilang:robin.html>Robin</a> Hood and other <a href = vnd.unilang:outlaws.html>Outlaws</a></a></cite>, published 1912, lines 29–34, page 98:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Then spake Much the milner son, / Ever more well him betide! / ‘Take twelve of thy <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> yeomen, / Well weapon’d by thy side. / Such one would thyselfë slon, / That twelve dare not abide.’</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="ante">a.</abbr></i> <b>1828</b>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leesome_Brand" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Leesome Brand">Leesome <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>Brand</a></a>”, in Buchan, <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a>, editor, <cite>Ancient Ballads and <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a> of the North of Scotland</cite>, volume 1, published 1828, lines 21–24, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=KT9Odv05vMcCamp;pg=PA39">page 39</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Ye do you to my father's stable, / Where <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> do stand baith <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></b> and able; / Strike ane <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>' them upo' the back, / The swiftest will gie his head a wap.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> (140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wéy-</i>, plural of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*éǵh₂</i>. ***wijd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijd.html>wijd</a> (5894)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijt.html>wijt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīdo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīdaz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:wied.html>wied</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wiid</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">weit</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wide</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">vid</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijd.html>wijd</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijder.html>wijder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">wijdst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wide</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijden.html>wijden</a> (11221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wiën</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīhijaną</i>. The <i>-d-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to hypercorrection (<a href = vnd.unilang:regarding.html>regarding</a> the frequent loss of intervocalic <i>-d-</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to dedicate, devote

***wijf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijf.html>wijf</a> (2628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijf.html>wijf</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wībą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijf.html>wijf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijven.html>wijven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijfje.html>wijfje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> woman, <span class="use-with-mention">potentially being as pejorative as</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Brabantian</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> Da <a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wijf.html>wijf</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ij.html>ij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> gu <a href = vnd.unilang:lige.html>lige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gat.html>gat</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a> really <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> advantage of <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:babe.html>babe</a>, broad</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The diminutive of this word <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an independent meaning (“female animal”). Colloquial diminutives (e.g. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wijfie</i>) often have a familiar meaning.
</p>

***wijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijk.html>wijk</a> (4881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wijc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wīk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīkō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vīcus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyḱ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village, household</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-wich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-wick</i>, archaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weich-</i> in <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weichbild</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">municipal area</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍅𐌴𐌹𐌷𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">weihs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīhsą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village, settlement</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> of the same Proto-Indo-European root.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijk.html>wijk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijken.html>wijken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijk.html>wijkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wile</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">while</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wīla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwīlō</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wile</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijle.html>wijle</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijn.html>wijn</a> (1167)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijn.html>wijn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*wīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vīnum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijn.html>wijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijnen.html>wijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijntje.html>wijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wine, an alcoholic beverage produced by a certain fermentation procedure; unless otherwise specified or indicated by context, made from <a href = vnd.unilang:grapes.html>grapes</a>.</li></ol>

***wijs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a> (1752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīsaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzer.html>wijzer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijst.html>wijst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wise</li>
<li>nice, fun (see usage notes)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Meaning 2 (nice, fun) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very popular in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/East_Flanders" class="extiw" title="w:East Flanders">East Flanders</a>, in the expression <i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:vree.html>vree</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>wijs</a>"</i>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***wijzen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijzen.html>wijzen</a> (2575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wisen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wīsen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīsijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzen.html>wijzen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to point
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wijs.html>Wijs</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anderen.html>anderen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onbeleefd.html>onbeleefd</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>point</b> at others, that's rude!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijl.html>pijl</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wijst.html>wijst</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:richting.html>richting</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dichtstbijzijnde.html>dichtstbijzijnde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooduitgang.html>nooduitgang</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The arrow <b>points</b> in the direction of the nearest emergency exit.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to point out, indicate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klok.html>klok</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wijst.html>wijst</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:twaalf.html>twaalf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The clock <b>indicates</b> twelve <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>'clock.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leraar.html>leraar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>wees</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leerlingen.html>leerlingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fouten.html>fouten</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The teacher <b>pointed out</b> their mistakes to the students.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>

***wijzer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijzer.html>wijzer</a> (8141)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzen.html>wijzen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzer.html>wijzer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzers.html>wijzers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijzertje.html>wijzertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***wikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wikken.html>wikken</a> (66541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wicken</i>, an intensive form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wēgen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to weigh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wikken.html>wikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to weigh
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to consider, ponder, weigh various options
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overdenken.html>overdenken</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overwegen.html>overwegen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The sense <i>to consider</i> or <i>ponder</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mostly used in the set phrase <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wikken.html>wikken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a></i> ("to consider carefully").

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wild</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"> singular past indicative and subjunctive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a></i></span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wou.html>wou</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weelde.html>weelde</a></i></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wildi</i>, a contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a> gi</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>).
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The contraction <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes reinforced with an additional <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, giving <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>

***wilderness.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> wilderness (5194)</h1><br></body> 
***wildernis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wildernis.html>wildernis</a> (7311)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wildernisse</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-nisse</i> (modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wild</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i>). The <i>-r-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> added by anology with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hindernis.html>hindernis</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duisternis.html>duisternis</a></i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wildnis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:willa.html>willa</a> (25509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiljô</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">willio</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">willo</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">willo</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wille.html>Wille</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">vili</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">vilja</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:willa.html>willa</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang">willan</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>desire, inclination, will
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latinx mention e-example" lang="ang">wilġesīþ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">willing companion</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latinx mention e-example" lang="ang">willwyrdan</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be complaisant</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>wish, desire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latinx mention e-example" lang="ang">wilcuma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">desired guest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>pleasure, delight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latinx mention e-example" lang="ang">wilboda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">angel, messenger of joy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>will, intent</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latinx" lang="ang">wilġesīþ</span></li>
<li><span class="Latinx" lang="ang">willian</span></li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a> (166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiljaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*welh₁-</i>. The variant spelling <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wouden.html>wouden</a></i> goes back to early <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wolde</i><i>(n)</i>, following the standard <i>ol</i> gt; <i>ou</i> transformation in Middle Dutch.
</p>

<ol><li>to want, to desire</li>

</p>
